Î“Ă¶Ă©  Plans global tab under the Draft sub-tab. Working from a recent draft can   Î“Ă¶Ă©

Î“Ă¶Ă©  Information, Part 2 \u2013 Auto Insurer Information, Part 3 \u2013 Other    Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  Insurer Information. (OCF-18.pdf p.5)\n\n5) Save drafts regularly\n- Click  Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  Save Draft periodically to store progress. This creates a draft on the      Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  Plans global tab under the Draft sub-tab. Working from a recent draft can   Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  save steps when creating new OCF-18s. Do not use drafts older than one      Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  year \u2014 delete drafts older than one year to avoid submission errors    Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  (old OCF versions are not compatible with AI). (OCF-18.pdf p.5)\n\n6)     Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  Complete signatures on Tab 2\n- On Tab 2 complete Part 4 (Signature of      Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  Health Practitioner). The OCF-18 cannot be submitted unless the answer to:  Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  \"Is the Health Practitioner certifying the plan also the Regulated Health  Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  Professional who is preparing and supervising the plan?\" is \"Yes.\" Use   Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  the drop-down calendar or type the date (YYYY/MM/DD) in the Signed Date     Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  field. (OCF-18.pdf p.13)\n- Select \"Yes\" if the Health Practitioner is    Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  in your Providers list and will supervise the Treatment Plan (then Part 5   Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  signature is not required). Select \"No\" if the Health Practitioner is in  Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  your Providers list but will not supervise the Treatment Plan (then Part 5  Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  is required). If the Health Practitioner who signed Part 4 is external to   Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  your facility, \"No\" will be selected automatically and Part 5 must be     Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  signed. (OCF-18.pdf p.13)\n- Ensure Part 5 (Signature of Regulated Health   Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  Professional) is signed when required by a Regulated Health Professional    Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  affiliated with your facility. FSRA business rules apply: Part 4 may be     Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  signed by a Health Practitioner not affiliated with your facility; Part 5   Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  must be signed by an affiliated Regulated Health Professional. (OCF-18.pdf  Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  p.13)\n\n7) Final review & submit\n- Review all entries, signatures and     Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  dates on the OCF-18. Submit the OCF-18 through AI when complete.          Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  (OCF-18.pdf p.4, p.13)\n\n8) If you need to invoice (OCF-21B)\n- To create  Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  an OCF-21B invoice from a submitted OCF-18: locate the submitted Plan on    Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  the applicable Plans tab, click the magnifying glass to open the Plan,      Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  then choose Create Invoice to open an OCF-21B. Many invoice fields will be  Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  populated from the submitted OCF-18 but remain editable. Alternatively,     Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  create an OCF-21B from scratch when no OCF-18 was previously submitted.     Î“Ă¶Ă©
Î“Ă¶Ă©  (OCF-21B.pdf p.4)\n\nNotes / Reminders\n- The OCF-18 is used for injuries   Î“Ă¶Ă©
